#Will check what ideas are already present. It will trigger an event for the next removal (probably faster than what was already rolled)
shared_focus = {
	id = FAT_anti_banditry_tactics
	icon = GFX_focus_FAT_anti_banditry_tactics
	prerequisite = { focus = FAT_pacify_the_countryside }
	x = 1
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = FAT_enforce_martial_law
	cost = 2
	ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FAT_anti_banditry_tactics"
		custom_effect_tooltip = FAT_reduce_banditry2_tp
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = FAT_Chaos_idea }
				country_event = {
					id = griffonRepublic.20
					days = 5
					random = 192					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = FAT_Chaos_idea1 }
				country_event = {
					id = griffonRepublic.21
					days = 7
					random = 480					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = griffonRepublic.22
					days = 7
					random = 480					#days to hours applied
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		x = -8
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = FAW_focus_suntail_empire
				has_country_flag = FAW_focus_suntail_empire_endgame
				has_country_flag = FAT_focus_iron_marshal
				has_country_flag = FAT_focus_civil_war
				has_country_flag = FAW_focus_empire_vassal
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 30 }
	available = {
		NOT = { has_idea = FAT_unruly_army_idea }
		has_civil_war = no
		hidden_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_idea = FAT_Army_Reform_idea2 }
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FAT_new_military"
		army_experience = 25
		add_command_power = 30
		FAT_army_dyn_mod_setup = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = FAT_Army_Reform_idea3
					has_idea = FAT_Army_Reform_idea4
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = FAT_roll_army_reform_into_dynmod_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
				add_to_variable = { FAT_max_planning = 0.10 }
				add_to_variable = { FAT_experience_gain_army_factor = 0.075 }
				add_to_variable = { FAT_conscription_factor = -0.05 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = FAT_Army_Reform_idea3 }
					remove_ideas = FAT_Army_Reform_idea3
					add_to_variable = { FAT_army_org_factor = 0.10 }
					add_to_variable = { FAT_land_reinforce_rate = 0.07 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = FAT_Army_Reform_idea4 }
					remove_ideas = FAT_Army_Reform_idea4
					add_to_variable = { FAT_army_org_factor = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { FAT_political_power_factor = 0.10 }
					add_to_variable = { FAT_army_morale_factor = 0.10 }
				}
			}
		}
		one_random_arms_factory = yes
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
}
